Publishing Your E-Commerce= Website

Here's a step-b= y-step guide to publish your TechHaven website online:

Option 1: Using Free Hosting Services (Simplest for Beginners)

  1. GitHub Pages (Free)

    • Create a GitHub account at github.c= om
    • Create a new repository named {yo= urusername}.github.io
    • Upload your HTML file (name it in= dex.html)
    • Push the file to your repository=
    • Your site will be live at https:/= /{yourusername}.github.io

  2. Netlify Drop (Free)

    • Go to netlify.com
    • Simply drag and drop your HTML file int= o the Netlify Drop zone
    • Your site will be instantly deployed wi= th a free netlify.app URL

Option 2: Using Paid Hosting (More Professional)

  1. Purchase a Domain Name

    • Popular registrars: Namecheap, Google D= omains, or GoDaddy ($10-15/year)

  2. Choose a Hosting Provider

    • Shared Hosting (cheape= st): Bluehost, SiteGround ($3-10/month)
    • VPS Hosting: DigitalOc= ean, Linode ($5-20/month)
    • Serverless: Vercel, Ne= tlify (free tier available)

  3. Upload Your Files

    • Use FTP (FileZilla) or your hosting pro= vider's file manager
    • Upload the HTML file as index.htm= l

Option 3: E-Commerce Platforms (Better for Real Stores)

  1. Shopify

    • Create account at shopify.com
    • Use their theme editor to implement you= r design
    • Add products and payment processing

  2. WordPress + WooCommerce

    • Install WordPress on your hosting
    • Add WooCommerce plugin
    • Either implement your design as a custo= m theme or use a page builder

Important Steps After Publishing

  1. Setup SSL Certificate (for HTT= PS)

    • Most hosting providers offer free Let's= Encrypt SSL

  2. Connect Your Domain (if using = custom domain)

    • Point DNS records to your hosting provi= der

  3. Test Your Site

    • Check on mobile and desktop devices
    • Test all links and interactive elements=

  4. Add Analytics

    • Google Analytics (free)
    • Or Plausible Analytics (privacy-focused= )
